***подбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбить.html>подби́ть</a> (7031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбить.html>подби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбивать.html>подбива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to line (lining)</li>
<li>to resole (shoes)</li>
<li>to damage, to hurt (e.g. a person's eye)</li>
<li>to shoot down (bird, airplane)</li>
<li>to instigate, to abet <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to assist or encourage in crime</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to assess, to sum up, to reckon up</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подбо́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podbój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***подбодрить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбодрить.html>подбодри́ть</a> (18759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодрить.html>бодри́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bodrítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбодрить.html>подбодри́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbodrítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подбодря́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбадривать.html>подба́дривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cheer up, to encourage</li></ol>

***подбора.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбора.html>подбо́ра</a> (14849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбора.html>подбо́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbóra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подборка.html>подбо́рка</a> (30877)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подобрать.html>подобра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podobrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on the nominal combining stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подбор-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podbor-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from the present tense stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подбер-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podber-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with Indo-European <i>o</i>-vocalization characteristic of deverbal nouns.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подборка.html>подбо́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подборка.html>подбо́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подборка.html>подбо́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подборка.html>подбо́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>selection, matching</li>
<li>pickup</li>
<li>selection, set, <i>(in a newspaper)</i> related items/stories</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывать.html>подбра́сывать</a> (8577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбросить.html>подбро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podbrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывать.html>подбра́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbrásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбросить.html>подбро́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to toss up, to throw up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывать.html>подбра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́х</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podbrásyvatʹ</b> rebjónka (na rukáx)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to toss up (dandle) a child</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to throw <i>(under)</i></li>
<li>to put secretly/stealthily, to plant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывать.html>подбра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podbrásyvatʹ</b> rebjónka komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to abandon a baby at someone's door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывать.html>подбра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наркотик.html>нарко́тики</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podbrásyvatʹ</b> narkótiki komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to plant drugs on someone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to add</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give (somebody) a lift (in a vehicle)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring up, to give some more
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывать.html>подбра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:резерв.html>резе́рвы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podbrásyvatʹ</b> rezérvy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw in one's reserves</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывающий.html>подбра́сывающий</a> (8577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывающий.html>подбра́сывающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbrásyvajuščij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбросить.html>подбро́сить</a> (6046)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросить.html>бро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбросить.html>подбро́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbrósitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбрасывать.html>подбра́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw upwards</li>
<li>to flip</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give (somebody) a lift (in a vehicle)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергнуть.html>подве́рг</a>(нуть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvérg(nutʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvergátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергнуть.html>подве́ргнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to subject (to), to expose (to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:суровый.html>суро́вой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:критика.html>кри́тике</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> suróvoj krítike</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to excoriate, to denounce</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опасность.html>опа́сности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> opásnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jeopardize</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> somnéniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to call into question</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штра́фу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> štrafu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fine</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:осмотр.html>осмо́тру</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> osmótru</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to examine, to subject to examination</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:испытание.html>испыта́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> ispytániju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put to the test, to put on trial</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> nakazániju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to impose a penalty <i>(upon)</i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:допрос.html>допро́су</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> doprósu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to interrogate, to examine, to question</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пытка.html>пы́тке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹ</b> pýtke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to subject to torture; to put on the rack</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвергаться.html>подверга́ться</a> (6580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvergátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергаться.html>подверга́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvergátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергнуться.html>подве́ргнуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to undergo, to be exposed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергаться.html>подверга́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствию</a> чего́-либо.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹsja</b> déjstviju čevó-libo.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be subject/subjected to something, to experience something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергаться.html>подверга́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:резкий.html>ре́зкой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:критика.html>кри́тике</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹsja</b> rézkoj krítike</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run the gauntlet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергаться.html>подверга́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опасность.html>опа́сности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹsja</b> opásnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run the risk <i>(of)</i>, to run the danger <i>(of)</i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергаться.html>подверга́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изучение.html>изуче́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹsja</b> izučéniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to receive the study</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергаться.html>подверга́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:унижение.html>униже́ниям</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvergátʹsja</b> unižénijam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to suffer indignity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvergátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***подвергнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвергнуть.html>подве́ргнуть</a> (10382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ве́ргнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vérgnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергнуть.html>подве́ргнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvérgnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергать.html>подверга́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to subject (to), to expose (to)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Formerly, the past passive participle was <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подверженный.html>подве́рженный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvéržennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which now functions only as an adjective.
</p>

***подвернуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуть.html>подверну́ть</a> (16503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуть.html>подверну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подвёртывать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подвора́чивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tighten, to screw a little further
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуть.html>подверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кран.html>кран</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvernútʹ</b> kran</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten up a tap</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуть.html>подверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:винт.html>винт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvernútʹ</b> vint</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tighten (take up) a screw</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tuck in, to tuck up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуть.html>подверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:одеяло.html>одея́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvernútʹ</b> odejálo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tuck in the blanket</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn up, to roll up</li>
<li>to sprain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуть.html>подверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvernútʹ</b> nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sprain one's ankle</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуться.html>подверну́ться</a> (9627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуть.html>подверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуться.html>подверну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvernútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подвёртываться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подвора́чиваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tuck up</li>
<li>to slip
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуться.html>подверну́лась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó nogá <b>podvernúlasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his foot slipped</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуться.html>подверну́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удобный.html>удо́бный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чай</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvernúlsja</b> udóbnyj slúčaj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">an opportunity turned up</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кстати.html>кста́ти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуться.html>подверну́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on kstáti <b>podvernúlsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he turned up just at the right moment</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>ве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвесить.html>подве́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvésitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвешивать.html>подве́шивать</a></b>)
